fs2:
* Stream has additional generic parameter (Task)
* Library code is very hard to read b/c of generic overuse:
  def ++[G[_],Lub[_],O2>:O](s2: => Stream[G,O2])(implicit R: RealSupertype[O,O2], L: Lub1[F,G,Lub]): Stream[Lub,O2] =
  def evalMap[G[_],Lub[_],O2](f: O => G[O2])(implicit L: Lub1[F,G,Lub]): Stream[Lub,O2] =

* Idea can't infer types in some places due to very complex generic params
(good code red w/o switching off type aware highlight, cant't show type of expression when using sequence etc)
* Scaladocs sucks (Task.parallelTraverse)

rxscala:
* Feels very imperative
* Lacking Task analog

Random thoughts:
* Try seems way cooler than Either[CustomError, Result]
** Handles thrown exceptions as well as "normal" errors
** No need to do this: Either.catchNonFatal{...}.leftMap(CustomError.fromThrowable)
** Gives you line numbers
** Much shorter


* get search keywords list from db
* for each keyword
** search tweets
** for each tweet fire request to analyzer server
** collect results: positive count, negative count, save this report to db
** for each positive tweet

rest crud api to manage search keywords list
